# Spectre
@Themida (1170804193339125871) sent me this source, and i have no use for it. I'm not sure how good it is or whether or not it works.
# Features
- MAC Address Spoofing

- HWID Serial Spoofing

- Network Spoofing
# Notes 
I was looking through it and noticed it attempts to disable security software, and modifies system registries. 

<img width="1208" height="344" alt="image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/d158febf-eff6-4704-9610-b3b60d4279c8" />

# MAC Address
```std::wstring MakCakm() {
    std::srand(static_cast<unsigned int>(std::time(nullptr)));
    const std::string hexChars = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    const std::string kamPrefix = "02"; 

    std::string mac = kamPrefix;
    mac += "-4B-41-4D";
    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mac += "-";
        for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
            mac += hexChars[std::rand() % hexChars.size()];
        }
    }
    std::transform(mac.begin(), mac.end(), mac.begin(), ::toupper);
    return std::wstring(mac.begin(), mac.end());
}

std::vector<std::wstring> GetPhysicalAdapterDeviceIDs() {
    std::vector<std::wstring> deviceIDs;

    HRESULT hres = CoInitializeEx(0, COINIT_MULTITHREADED);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Failed to initialize COM library. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    hres = CoInitializeSecurity(
        NULL,
        -1,
        NULL,
        NULL,
        RPC_C_AUTHN_LEVEL_DEFAULT,
        RPC_C_IMP_LEVEL_IMPERSONATE,
        NULL,
        EOAC_NONE,
        NULL
    );

    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Failed to initialize security. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        CoUninitialize();
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    IWbemLocator* pLoc = NULL;
    hres = CoCreateInstance(
        CLSID_WbemLocator,
        0,
        CLSCTX_INPROC_SERVER,
        IID_IWbemLocator,
        (LPVOID*)&pLoc
    );

    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Failed to create IWbemLocator object. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        CoUninitialize();
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    IWbemServices* pSvc = NULL;
    hres = pLoc->ConnectServer(
        _bstr_t(L"ROOT\\CIMV2"),
        NULL,
        NULL,
        0,
        NULL,
        0,
        0,
        &pSvc
    );

    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Could not connect to WMI. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    hres = CoSetProxyBlanket(
        pSvc,
        RPC_C_AUTHN_WINNT,
        RPC_C_AUTHZ_NONE,
        NULL,
        RPC_C_AUTHN_LEVEL_CALL,
        RPC_C_IMP_LEVEL_IMPERSONATE,
        NULL,
        EOAC_NONE
    );

    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Could not set proxy blanket. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        pSvc->Release();
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    IEnumWbemClassObject* pEnumerator = NULL;
    hres = pSvc->ExecQuery(
        bstr_t("WQL"),
        bstr_t("SELECT DeviceID FROM Win32_NetworkAdapter WHERE PhysicalAdapter=TRUE"),
        WBEM_FLAG_FORWARD_ONLY | WBEM_FLAG_RETURN_IMMEDIATELY,
        NULL,
        &pEnumerator
    );

    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        LI_FN(system)(E("cls"));
        std::cerr << "Query for physical adapters failed. Error code: " << hres << std::endl;
        pSvc->Release();
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return deviceIDs;
    }

    IWbemClassObject* pclsObj = NULL;
    ULONG uReturn = 0;

    while (pEnumerator) {
        hres = pEnumerator->Next(WBEM_INFINITE, 1, &pclsObj, &uReturn);
        if (uReturn == 0) break;

        VARIANT vtProp;
        hres = pclsObj->Get(L"DeviceID", 0, &vtProp, 0, 0);
        if (SUCCEEDED(hres)) {
            deviceIDs.push_back(vtProp.bstrVal);
            VariantClear(&vtProp);
        }
        pclsObj->Release();
    }

    pSvc->Release();
    pLoc->Release();
    pEnumerator->Release();
    CoUninitialize();

    return deviceIDs;
}

bool SetRegistryMACValue(const std::wstring& deviceID, const std::wstring& macAddress) {
    std::wstring basePath = L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Class\\{4D36E972-E325-11CE-BFC1-08002BE10318}\\";
    std::wstring prefixes[] = { L"", L"0", L"00", L"000" };

    for (const auto& prefix : prefixes) {
        std::wstring fullPath = basePath + prefix + deviceID;

        HKEY hKey;
        LONG result = RegOpenKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, fullPath.c_str(), 0, KEY_WRITE, &hKey);
        if (result == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
            result = RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"NetworkAddress", 0, REG_SZ,
                (const BYTE*)macAddress.c_str(),
                (macAddress.size() + 1) * sizeof(wchar_t));
            RegCloseKey(hKey);

            if (result == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                return true;
            }
        }
    }

    return false;
}
static size_t WriteCallback(void* contents, size_t size, size_t nmemb, std::string* s) {
    size_t newLength = size * nmemb;
    s->append((char*)contents, newLength);
    return newLength;
}

bool DisablePowerSaving(const std::wstring& deviceID) {
    std::wstring basePath = L"SYSTEM\\CurrentControlSet\\Control\\Class\\{4D36E972-E325-11CE-BFC1-08002BE10318}\\";
    std::wstring prefixes[] = { L"", L"0", L"00", L"000" };
    DWORD pnpCapabilities = 24;

    for (const auto& prefix : prefixes) {
        std::wstring fullPath = basePath + prefix + deviceID;

        HKEY hKey;
        LONG result = RegOpenKeyExW(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, fullPath.c_str(), 0, KEY_WRITE, &hKey);
        if (result == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
            result = RegSetValueExW(hKey, L"PnPCapabilities", 0, REG_DWORD,
                (const BYTE*)&pnpCapabilities, sizeof(DWORD));
            RegCloseKey(hKey);

            if (result == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
                return true;
            }
        }
    }

    return false;
}

void ResetNetworkAdapters() {
    HRESULT hres = CoInitializeEx(0, COINIT_MULTITHREADED);
    if (FAILED(hres)) return;

    hres = CoInitializeSecurity(NULL, -1, NULL, NULL, RPC_C_AUTHN_LEVEL_DEFAULT,
        RPC_C_IMP_LEVEL_IMPERSONATE, NULL, EOAC_NONE, NULL);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        CoUninitialize();
        return;
    }

    IWbemLocator* pLoc = NULL;
    hres = CoCreateInstance(CLSID_WbemLocator, 0, CLSCTX_INPROC_SERVER,
        IID_IWbemLocator, (LPVOID*)&pLoc);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        CoUninitialize();
        return;
    }

    IWbemServices* pSvc = NULL;
    hres = pLoc->ConnectServer(_bstr_t(L"ROOT\\CIMV2"), NULL, NULL, 0, NULL, 0, 0, &pSvc);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return;
    }

    hres = CoSetProxyBlanket(pSvc, RPC_C_AUTHN_WINNT, RPC_C_AUTHZ_NONE, NULL,
        RPC_C_AUTHN_LEVEL_CALL, RPC_C_IMP_LEVEL_IMPERSONATE, NULL, EOAC_NONE);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        pSvc->Release();
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return;
    }

    IEnumWbemClassObject* pEnumerator = NULL;
    hres = pSvc->ExecQuery(bstr_t("WQL"),
        bstr_t("SELECT NetConnectionID FROM Win32_NetworkAdapter WHERE NetConnectionID IS NOT NULL"),
        WBEM_FLAG_FORWARD_ONLY | WBEM_FLAG_RETURN_IMMEDIATELY,
        NULL, &pEnumerator);
    if (FAILED(hres)) {
        pSvc->Release();
        pLoc->Release();
        CoUninitialize();
        return;
    }

    IWbemClassObject* pclsObj = NULL;
    ULONG uReturn = 0;

    while (pEnumerator) {
        hres = pEnumerator->Next(WBEM_INFINITE, 1, &pclsObj, &uReturn);
        if (uReturn == 0) break;

        VARIANT vtProp;
        hres = pclsObj->Get(L"NetConnectionID", 0, &vtProp, 0, 0);
        if (SUCCEEDED(hres)) {
            std::wstring interfaceName = vtProp.bstrVal;

            std::wstring disableCmd = L"netsh interface set interface name=\"" + interfaceName + L"\" disable";
            std::wstring enableCmd = L"netsh interface set interface name=\"" + interfaceName + L"\" enable";

            _wsystem(disableCmd.c_str());
            _wsystem(enableCmd.c_str());

            VariantClear(&vtProp);
        }
        pclsObj->Release();
    }

    pSvc->Release();
    pLoc->Release();
    pEnumerator->Release();
    CoUninitialize();
}
```
